His outburst helped Utah overcome a quarter in which Cleveland blocked five shots and the Jazz totaled only five baskets.,''I was just being aggressive in those moments,'' Clarkson said. ''Throughout the game, I saw what they were doing defensively and just started being aggressive in the fourth.'',Mitchell kept the Cavaliers' offense afloat in the first half while his teammates struggled to find their shot.
